ministerio publico brasileiro combate aquecimento global the role of brazilian prosecutors in combating global warming vinicius lameira bernardo1 1 promotor justica ministerio publico estado rio janeiro especialista gestao passivos ambientais cepeduerj llm direito publico enfase meio am biente universidade melbourneaustralia professor escola governo mprj ierrb politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 31 resumo presente capitulo objetivo debater papel ministerio pu blico combate aquecimento global inicialmente apresentamos lei tor conceitos cientificos basicos fenomeno mudancas climaticas bem causas consequencias sistemas naturais humanos quencia capitulo examina razao extrai ordenamento juri dico brasileiro dever poder publico combater fenomeno aque cimento global adotando medidas mitigacao adaptacao finalmente capitulo aborda estrategias atuacao membros ministerio publico tanto campo medidas mitigadoras quanto adaptativas forma fo mentar acao setor publico privado area mudancas climaticas palavraschave mudancas climaticas aquecimento global meio am biente ministerio publico litigancia climatica abstract this paper aims to discuss how brazilian prosecutors may act in defense of healthy climate system combating global warming to so it initially provides an overview of the science behind climate change discussing its causes and consequences to human and natural systems in sequence the paper examines how brazilian legal framework supports the assertion that brazilian government must act on the field of climate chan ge puting in place mitigation and adptation measures finally the paper examines how prosecoturs may act to combat global warming approaching strategies of mitigation and adaptation in order to foster further action from public and private estagnacao metas relacionadas ods reduzidos avancos im plementacao politica nacional mudancas clima desmonte brasil relevantes orgaos ambientais enfraquecendo acoes dirigidas combater mudancas adversos aquecimento global palavraschave agenda 2030 objetivos desenvolvimento sustenta vel mudancas climaticas ministerio publico abstract the present study analyses the effective fulfillment of the 2030 agenda and the sus tainable development goals in the context of climate change sdg 13 in view of the international commitments brazil has made aiming at taking adaptation mitigation and resilience measures associated to global warming recent technical data has revea led worsening in the world scenario involving climate change the stagnation of the targets related to the sdgs diminished advances in the implementation of the national policy on climate change and the dismantling of relevant environmental organizations in brazil weakening the actions directed to combating climate changes and their im pacts finally the study addresses the relevant role of the public prosecutors office in the inspection and implementation of the national policy on climate change and sdgs on combating climate change cristina seixas graca1 1 mestre direito universidade federal bahia ufba especialista direito ambiental contra mudancas climati cas esgotamento recursos universidad castillala mancha promotora justica ministerio publico estado bahia membro auxiliar cnmp presidente associacao brasileira membros ministerio publico meio am biente abrampa professora politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 74 resumo tratase analise tendencia retrocessos niveis protecao ambiental vem ocorrendo brasil correlacao atendimento compromissos sustentabilidade assumidos tratados interna cionais principalmente quanto metas reducao gee propostas acordo paris conformidade parametros tecnicos cientificos contencao mudancas climaticas efeitos governanca ambiental fraca desorientada ordenamento juridico protetivo sinaliza des cumprimento metas assumidas potencializa novas catastrofes piores condicoes vida presentes futuras geracoes impedindo ideal desenvolvimento sustentavel existencia digna palavrachave retrocesso ambiental abstract this is an analysis of the trend of setbacks in the levels of environmental protection which has been occurring in brazil and its correlation with meeting the commitments to sustainability assumed in international treaties mainly regarding the ghg reduction targets proposed in the paris agreement and in accordance with the scientific technical parameters containing climate change and its effects the weak and disoriented en vironmental governance of the most protective legal system signals the noncompliance with the goals that have been undertaken and potentialize new catastrophes and worse living conditions present and future generations impeding the ideal of sustainable development and dignified existence mudancas climaticas acao 92 resumo presente artigo trata responsabilidade civil danos associados mudancas climaticas tanto perspectiva preventiva reparato ria inicialmente propoe caracterizacao desses danos cumulativos seguida analisa alternativas teoricas termos imputacao res ponsabilidade fim indica hipoteses responsabilidade civil apoio desenvolvimento ambito direito ambiental pode ter aplicacao promissora justica brasileira palavraschave responsabilidade civil danos cumulativos litigios cli maticos abstract the article deals with civil liability damages associated with climate change both in its preventive and reparative perspective it starts with the characterization of these damages cumulative damages and afterwards it analyzes theoretical alternatives in terms of imputation it concludes with the indication of hypotheses in which civil liability supported by its development in the scope of environmental law can have promising application in brazilian law keywords civil senao maior importancia ja trata continuidade vida terra direito mundo assiste passagem direito simbolico protecao contra mudancas climaticas direito levado serio ocorrido meio chamados litigios climaticos crescimento exponencial deste tipo demanda diversos paises ja originou decisoes emblematicas tribunais estrangeiros chegou brasil onde recentes processos geram expectativa pronunciamento litigio climati co jurisprudencia abstract climate change is one of the most relevant topics today if not the most important since it is about the continuity of life on earth in law the world is witnessing the tran sition from symbolic right to protection against climate change to right taken seri ously which has occurred through socalled climate litigation the exponential growth of this type of demand in several countries has already led to emblematic decisions in foreign courts and has reached brazil where recent lawsuits generate the expectation of pronouncement by national courts including in the brazilian supreme court this arti cle aims to analyze some of the main precedents of foreign and brazilian jurisprudence keywords environmental law climate changes climatic litigation ambiente ja considerado tema trans versal perpassar todas atividades humanas acrescentase agora aspecto climatico transversal todas dimensoes ambientais microbem macrobem ambiental crescimento exponencial demandas climaticas originou decisoes emblematicas tribunais estrangeiros modo timido porem nao desprovido relevancia chegou brasil onde recentes processos geram expectativa pronunciamento direito fundacao escola superior mi nisterio publico pesquisadora foco direito ani obra norberto bobbio politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 135 resumo tendo vista importancia atualidade discussao sobre mudancas climaticas mostrase necessario compreender criticamente instrumentos politica ambiental adequados mitigacao efeitos mudancas climaticas presente artigo objetiva analisar uso instrumentos eco nomicos nesse contexto tanto busca compreender circunstancias historicas criacao direito ambiental nacional internacional instru mentos politica ambiental relacao direito ambiental economia tambem analisa especificamente mecanismo desenvolvimento limpo mdl gerador certificados reducao emissoes creditos carbo instrumentos leis 121872009 141192021 conclui subssistemas direito ambiental economico sao interligados maior efetividade estados devem adotar politicas ambientais eficientes adequadas fins propostos fim entende teoria ordenamento deve revisitada dar condicoes uso instrumentos economicos palavraschave mudancas climaticas politica ambiental instrumentos economicos funcao promocional direito abstract in view of the importance and timeliness of the discussion on climate change it is necessary to understand critically which environmental policy instruments are most suitable mitigating the effects of climate change this article aims to analyze the use of economic instruments in this context to this end it seeks to understand the his torical context of the creation of national and international environmental law the re lationship between environmental law and economics and the instruments of environ mental policy it specifically analyzes the clean development mechanism cdm the generator of emission reduction certificates carbon credits and the instruments of law n 121872009 and law n 141192021 it concludes that the subsystems of the environmental and economic law are interlinked and that greater effectiveness states must adopt policies that are defined the purposes proposed and that are effi cient finally that the ordering theory must be revisited to give conditions to the use of economic instruments keywords climate change environmental nacional meio ambiente politica nacional mudan cas climaticas direito ambiental abstract the article seeks to demonstrate that the direct insertion of the effective and poten tial damages and impacts of anthropic interference on the climate system in the envi ronmental licensing agenda of activities and undertakings endowed with significant degrading or polluting potential of the environment is one of the main ways to give effectiveness to the federal law that instituted the national policy on climate change keywords climate changes environmental licensing environmental impact stu dy and concerned with presenting panel on climate change law on the international stage in brazil and in the federal district it started from the legal fra meworks in these three areas and sought to diagnose the main challenges and action strategies with the citation of cases already processed in different courts and the results of some of them the legal nature of human and fundamental rights of the visao geral panorama bra sileiro relacao geracao destinacao residuos solidos pretendese demonstrar urgencia acoes integradas voltadas implementacao principios objetivos instrumentos politica nacional residuos solidos lei 1230510 bem importancia ministerio publico consecucao desses resultados decorrer texto serao trazidas ainda algumas reflexoes acerca estrategias politicas publicas am bientais podem contribuir enfrentamento mudancas climaticas desenvolvimento sustentavel palavraschave residuos solidos mudancas climaticas logistica reversa abstract this study aims to provide brief explanation about the relevance of solid waste ma nagement in the context of climate change and consequently of the need effective measures to reduce greenhouse gas emissions in this sector and contribute to meeting the international commitments and goals assumed by brazil by presenting an overview of the brazilian panorama with regard to the generation and disposal of solid waste the intention is to demonstrate the urgency of integrated actions aimed at implemen ting the principles objectives and instruments of the national solid waste policy law n 1230510 and on the importance of the public prosecutors office to achieve these results reading through the text gives rise to number of reflections on how these en vironmental strategies and public policies can contribute to tackling climate change and sustainable development keywords solid waste climate changes reverse logistic politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 228 1 introducao segundo panorama residuos solidos abstract this article analyzes the contribution of the solid waste project legal disposal to mitigate climate change the intersectoral action was developed by the public prosecu tors office of mato grosso sul in partnership with the court of auditors and the en vironment institute of mato grosso sul the objective of the project was to reduce the disposal of solid waste in illegal open dumpsites in the 79 municipalities of mato grosso sul legislation on solid waste and climate change is presented simulation methods on greenhouse gas emissions especially methane from landfills and open dumpsites are described the emission of carbon dioxide co2 due to the transshipment of solid waste between municipalities is calculated finally in case study this methodology is applied to the mato grosso sul state from 2016 to 2020 there was reduction from 63 80 to 16 20 municipalities with illegal open dumpsites and 45 municipalities started to send their solid waste to landfills these results show the contribution of this modification mitigation in climate change keywords solid waste sanitary landfill greenhouse effect climate change en vironment and public health intersectoral urbano ministerio publico abstract this article aims to evaluate the work of the public prosecutors office in relation to the interface generated by the formation of urban centers and the causes and effects of climate change and the role of planning the vulnerability of urban centers especially informal ones requires the public ministry to act more dynamic multidisciplinary and supportive based not only on legal knowledge but other areas including the use of geographic information systems gis from photographs and georeferenced descrip tions to vector maps this article addresses the concern with the development of cities linked to sustainability guidelines in order to use urban planning way to mitigate and adapt to the effects of climate change keywords climate change urban planning public ministry politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 282 1 introducao mudancas climaticas sao desafio precedentes escala global portanto enfrentamento exige participacao sociedade civil organizada poder publico sentido conservacao patrimonio natural pais implementacao politicas efetivas mitigacao adaptacao cresci mento acelerado concentrado populacao centros urbanos constitui si multaneamente principais fatores desencadeiam alteracoes clima tornam individuos extremamente fragilizados relacao im pactos dessas mesmas alteracoes nesse sentido sustentabilidade elevada categoria grande desafio ambiental atualidade planejamento urbano presente artigo objetivo entao analisar impactos sis tema climatico ocasionados crescimento desordenado cidades avaliando instrumentos serem incorporados planejamento urbano assim pretende contribuir elementos estrategicos governanca am biental mitigacao adaptacao mudancas climaticas tanto utilizase breve introducao sobre relacao cidades meio biotico geografia impactos mudancas climaticas partir regime juridico delineado lei politica nacional sobre mudanca clima lei reurb estatuto cidade sequencia tratase planejamento urbano diretrizes susten taveis licenciamento ambiental autorizacao procedimentos parcelamento solo regularizacao fundiaria moradias ati vidades potencial degradador poluidor meio ambiente avaliase ainda importancia uso ferramentas sistema informacao geografica outros bancos dados disponibilizados acesso tam bem necessaria sistematizacao elementos diretrizes planejamento urbano mitigar adaptar cidades mudancas climaticas abordase fim aprimoramento atuacao ministerio publico consequentemente politicas publicas setoriais relacionadas regularida urbanistica contribuem minimizar impactos causados mudancas climaticas politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 283 2 mudancas climaticas causas efeitos cidade mudancas previstas clima global devem impactar consideravelmen assentamentos humanos principalmente urbanos sobretudo in formais cidades modo funcionamento nesse cenario papel bastante relevante ja concentram principais fontes geradoras gases efeito estufa bem constituem locais maior ameaca riscos logo exigem seriedade discussao sobre alteracoes climaticas tanto perspectiva mitigacao quanto adaptacao estabilidade climatica regioes estacoes definidas condicoes amenas temperatura permitiu expansao civilizacoes surgimento primeiras cidades justamente faixa mesma latitude deslocamento humano desenvolvimento globo ocorreram forma intensa portanto sentido lesteoeste razao manutencao mesmas cir cunstancias climaticas vez sentido nortesul implicava mudanca brusca temperatura condicoes geograficas forma convivencia sociedade termos politica religiao tambem expandiu rapidamente mesma latitude modo civilizacoes surgiram compartilhando mes novas tecnicas agricolas caca mesmos equipamentos utensilios domesticos toda qualquer invencao inclusive modelos aldeias vilas cujas moradias infraestrutura modelavamse geografia comple mentandose pode denominar urbanismo biomorfico necessidade novas areas homo sapiens iniciou conquista regioes inospitas gelidas deserticas secas umidas lenta progressao permitiu adaptabilidade tanto sentido biologico alteracao proprio organismo nova realidade imposta naturalmente ambiente quanto incremento novos meios vestir habitar locomover alimentar presenca frio intenso neve impos transforma coes modos plantio visavam aumentar producao conserva cao embora diminuissem frequencia semeadura ocorreu locais montanhosos exigiram criatividade fixar moradia plantar estiagens excesso chuvas moldaram ambiente consequentemente tipos vilas habitacoes ocupacao espacos extremos planeta exigiu mitigacao efeitos climaticos diversos alterando forma viver sociedade adaptarse sempre constante especie humana porem adaptacao antes ocorria forma equilibrada gradual hoje impera improviso descredito politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 284 apesar grande diversidade fatores promoveram surgimen to desenvolvimento cidades possibilidade exploracao sustento obtencao lucro parece ter sido razoes signifi cativas fenomeno tendencia capitalista determinou surgimento vilas cidades longo tempo habitantes vez definiram usos razoes existir moldando estilo arquitetura estrutura seguranca conforto busca qualidade vida si ali residiam evoluiram sob varias perspectivas social economica urbanistica religiosa antropologica entanto principal necessidade refugio protecao intemperies predadores3 partir entao casas territorios passaram formar novos habitats vez caracterizam lugares convivencia espaco urbano hoje chamamos cidades nesse sentido podese dizer desenvolvimento destas inevitavel fruto constantes revolucoes sempre sustentaveis exemplo indus trial4 trouxe novos caminhos conversao energia producao bens servicos 2 diamond jared colapso 12 ed rio janeiro record 2020 p 24 3 casa territorio sao correlativos fundem maneira menos eficiente formar chamado habitat onde comunidades humanas encontram recursos necessarios existencia passado escolha local consertar casa dependia condicoes seguranca condicoes naturais een fim direitos humanos palavraschave mudanca climatica pantanal cerrado ministerio publico abstract the substantial changes in the climate in the brazilian pantanal and cerrado region have been felt and measured by experts whose phenomenon acts in the degradation of social and economic conditions of life adapted to less aggressive cycles which is enhan ced by the disorderly and hungry anthropization of spaces reproduction of economic activities without concern environmental sustainability primarily agropastoral the routine artifice of the fragmented study of enterprises and phenomena usually used by politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 326 the environmental aggressor and his official protector administrative or judicial pre vents responsible integrated view of the natural consequences flora wildlife and humans the set of socioenvironmental analyses on deforestation and forest fires example includes the imperative of studies on climate change the necessarily protective reaction which is expected from government institutions requires clear and commit ted discourse on the effects of climate change on social organization and its economic activities within which the brazilian public prosecutors office in the exercise of its cons titutional activity this intervention calls militant desire that becomes consistent with the awareness of the real and the duty to act truly contributing to the realization of environmental rights and by mandatory extension of social economic and cultural rights in short human rights keywords climate change pantanal publico brasileiro defesa meio ambiente ministerio publico abstract the national policy on climate change was instituted with the scope of establishing the planning management and mitigation of the causes and consequences of climate change actions to achieve natural climate variability include the preservation of natu ral resources way to prevent the depletion of the planet in order to advance in the implementation of the pnmc it is everyones duty to act the benefit of present and future generations to reduce the impacts resulting from unnatural climate interference being the duty of all the government and civil society this study aims to analyze how the environment committee of the national council of the public ministry developed in 2020 articulation actions between national state and municipal institutions in addition to civil society in order to strengthen the constitutional role of the public prosecutor in this area prescribed by the pnmc keywords environment commission of crescido cada dia brasil desde 29 dezembro 2009 ha dez anos existe lei federal 121872009 instituiu politica nacional mudanca clima pnmc fato incontroverso embora alguns insistam tese negacio nista aquecimento global problema mundial decorre cha mados gases efeito estufa gee dentre quais principal vilao segundo ciencia gas carbonico co2 concorrendo aproximadamente 75 efeito estufa solos subsolos acordo legislacao brasi leira sao considerados recursos ambientais co2 presente recurso ambiental solo potencial levando conta tamanho brasil sequestrar torno 40 citado gee dessa forma tutela so los deve obedecer aptidao capacidade suporte resiliencia deste ecossistema condao contribuir forma efetiva combate mudancas clima tambem melhoria generalizada servicos ecossistemicos funcoes ecologicas produzidas citado recurso am biental modo gerar beneficios sociais ambientais economicos palavraschave mudanca clima meio ambiente tutela solo gas efeito estufa abstract the theme of climate change has grown every day in brazil since december 29 2009 that is more than ten years there is the federal law 121872009 which instituted the national climate change policy pnmc it is an uncontroversial fact although some insist on the denialist thesis that global warming is global problem and stems from the socalled greenhouse gases ghg among which according to science is carbon dio xide co2 competing with approximately 75 the greenhouse effect soils and subsoils according to brazilian legislation are considered environmental resources co2 is present in the soil environmental resource which has the potential leading to the size of brazil of sequestration around 40 of the aforementioned ghg thus the protection of soils which must comply with the aptitude support capacity and resilience of that ecosystem has the power to contribute effectively to the combating of climate change and the widespread improvement of ecosystem services and ecological functions produced by aforementioned environmental resource bringing social environmental and economic benefits keywords climate change environment guardianship soil greenhouse gas politica nacional mudancas climaticas mitigation fundamental step towards restoration of degraded pastures is the identification and accurate mapping of these areas in brazil the area of degraded pastures is immense and therefore remote sensing is costeffective way to map it in this study an improved meth od based on ndvi values extracted from satellite images is presented and tested in the environmental protection area of uberaba river basin epaurb located in the state of minas gerais brazil the epaurb covers an area of approximately 5281 km2 509 of which is pasture the in novative features of this method comprise 1 the mapping is preceded by the definition of ndvi fingerprints healthy smoothly degraded moderately degraded and degraded pasture called physiognomies based on non linear relationships between ndvi values and time 2 the mapping of physiognomies accounts the influence of geology and weather seasonality on the ndvi values in the epaurb the physi ognomic categories were set by visual inspection and evaluation of soil politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 382 characteristics eg organic matter nutrients resistance to penetration in the socalled characterization ground truth sites also termed buffers resistance to penetration and several other soil parameters showed statistically different p005 values among physiognomies the defini tion of fingerprints was based on 4year record 20132016 of ndvi 16day composite mod13q1 250m timeseries data the map of graded pastures was delineated on the basis of comparisons between the ndvi values of 23 satellite images covering the year of 2016 termed ndvipixel and corresponding characteristic ndvi values of degrad ed pasture physiognomy extracted from the corresponding fingerprint termed ndvibuffer whenever ndvibuffermin ndvipixel ndvi buffermax repetition counter n increased one unit n3 the pixel was classified degraded pasture the results exposed 1601 km2 of degraded pasture 3n18 which represents 60 of all pasture land the areas mapped degraded pasture were subject to field check in 38 socalled validation ground truth sites using resistance to pene tration validation parameter with 841 success given the serious environmental damage posed by pasture degradation several mitiga tion measures were discussed including the protection of degraded soil through the polluter pays principle 22 22 degradacao pastagens representa problema estudo parte revisao bibliografica orientada teoricamente referencial poscolonial descolonial analisar concepcao con servacionista contexto mudancas climaticas pode afetar restringir direitos povos indigenas tanto apresentouse categoria colo nialidade ressaltando estrategias discurso colonial especial fixa cao estereotipo mecanismos manejados classificar restringir possibilidades compreensao atuacao transformacao pessoas gru pos tracado aporte teorico contextualizouse participacao indigena ambito convencaoquadro nacoes unidades sobre mudancas clima ticas cqnumc destaque previsoes acordo paris formalizacao participacao indigena contituencies fim tratouse entrelacamento conservacionismo discurso colonial consideran exemplos politicas nacionais conservacao relacionados mudancas climaticas pontuando relacao regularizacao terras indigenas mudancas climaticas concluiuse referido discurso reproduz logica colonialidade estrategia fixidez estereotipo tal tratado bhabha analisar discurso colonial simplificando amplas comple xas possibilidade interacao adaptacao modos vida indigenas face mudancas climaticas palavraschave colonialidade povos indigenas mudancas climaticas terras indigenas conservacionismo abstract this study uses the bibliographic review theoretically guided by the postcolonial and decolonial framework to analyze how the conservationist conception in the context of climate change can affect and restrict the rights of indigenous peoples to this end the category of coloniality was presented emphasizing the strategies of colonial discourse especially the fixation and stereotype mechanisms managed to classify and restrict the possibilities of understanding acting and transforming people and groups hav ing drawn up the theoretical contribution indigenous participation was contextualized within the united nations framework convention on climate change unfccc with emphasis on the paris agreement and the formalization of indigenous participation by contituencies finally the intertwining between conservationism and colonial discourse politica nacional mudancas climaticas acao 391 was presented considering examples and national conservation policies related to cli mate change and punctuating the relationship between regularization of indigenous lands and climate change it was concluded that the referred speech reproduces the logic of coloniality through the strategy of fixity and stereotype treated by bhabha when analyzing the colonial speech simplifying the wide and complex possibilities of interaction adaptation and 130 30 diegues ac enciclopedia caicara olhar pesquisador sao paulo hucitec 2004 31 section 2a in order to assure that an increasing population accompanied by expanding settlement and growing mechanization does not occupy and modify all areas within the uni ted states and its possessions leaving lands designated preservation and protection in their natural condition it is hereby declared to be the policy of the congress to secure the american people of present and future generations the benefits of an enduring resource of wil derness this purpose there is hereby established national wilderness preservation system to be composed of federally owned areas designated by congress wilderness areas and these shall be administered the use and enjoyment of the american people in such manner will leave them unimpaired future use and enjoyment wilderness and so to provide the protection of these areas the preservation of their wilderness character and the gathering and dissemination of information regarding their use and enjoyment wilderness and federal lands shall be designated wilderness areas except provided in this act or by subsequent act 32 definition of wilderness c wilderness in contrast with those areas where man and his own works dominate the landscape is hereby recognized an area where the earth and its community of life are untrammeled by man where man himself is visitor who does not remain an area of wilderness is further defined to mean in this act an area of undeveloped federal land retaining its primeval character and influence without permanent
